-----------------

Optimization Suggestions:
-------------------------
1. Focus on functions with high cumulative time in the cProfile output.
2. Look for unexpected function calls or loops that might be optimized.
3. Consider using more efficient data structures or algorithms where applicable.
4. Check for any I/O operations that could be optimized or made asynchronous.
5. Investigate memory usage patterns and optimize for lower memory consumption.
